	Hydra.ActorPlaySimpleConversation("QST_Hell_Ambush_1", Neyrelle_Prava, Donan_Prava)

	local tAmbushesIfPlayerRunsAhead = Hydra.ActorsInGroup("QST_Hell_Battlefield_AmbushesIfPlayerRunsAhead");
		
	if (#tAmbushesIfPlayerRunsAhead > 0) then
		for i, idAmbushActor in ipairs(tAmbushesIfPlayerRunsAhead) do
			Hydra.ActorDelete(idAmbushActor);
		end
	end
	
	Hydra.EventSend("ArtilleryAmbushOne")
	
	local tMeteorsLocations = Hydra.ActorsInGroup("QST_Hell_Bombardment_Marker_1");
	ShuffleTable(tMeteorsLocations)
	local flTotalDuration = 10;
	
	for i, idMeteor in ipairs(tMeteorsLocations) do 
		Hydra.ActorTriggerPowerAtFeet(idMeteor, "QST_Hell_Main_Meteor")
		Hydra.Wait(flTotalDuration/#tMeteorsLocations);
	end

</td></tr><tr><td><b>unk_b185921</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>unk_9c1ea4f</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>arLevelAreas</b></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><b>arSubzones</b></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><b>dwFlags</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>szOnCallbackCompleteScript</b></td><td><pre>function Start(idActor, idActorDetector)

followerLorath = Hydra.QuestGetFollower("NPC_QST_Lorath_Follower")
followerDonan = Hydra.QuestGetFollower("NPC_QST_Donan_Follower_Horadrim")
followerNeyrelle = Hydra.QuestGetFollower("NPC_QST_Neyrelle_Follower_OneArmed")


-- Lorath follower runs to his static place
				Hydra.QuestFollowerTakeOwnership(followerLorath)
				Hydra.ActorEnableAI(followerLorath, false)
				Hydra.QActorMoveToLocationDynamicSpeed(followerLorath, Lorath_Horde, "NPC_Run", true)
				Hydra.QActorFaceSameAsActor(followerLorath, Lorath_Horde)
				
-- Donan follower runs to his static place		
				Hydra.QuestFollowerTakeOwnership(followerDonan)
				Hydra.ActorEnableAI(followerDonan, false)
				Hydra.QActorMoveToLocationDynamicSpeed(followerDonan, Donan_Horde, "NPC_Run", true)
				Hydra.QActorFaceSameAsActor(followerDonan, Donan_Horde)
				
-- Neyrelle follower runs to her static place
				Hydra.QuestFollowerTakeOwnership(followerNeyrelle)
				Hydra.ActorEnableAI(followerNeyrelle, false)
				Hydra.QActorMoveToLocationDynamicSpeed(followerNeyrelle, Neyrelle_Horde, "NPC_Run", true)
				Hydra.QActorFaceSameAsActor(followerNeyrelle, Neyrelle_Horde)
